<div id="review_2242116211" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2242116211" />
    <a title="Katerina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina"><img alt="Katerina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470667070p2/5014021.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2242116211?book_show_action=true">Jan 04, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=science-fiction">science-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=2018-reads">2018-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2242116211" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11357555011677154006"><b>What do you live for? </b><br/><br/>Money? Fame? Glory? Love? Family? Ambition? <br/>For the autumn leaves that rustle under your feet? For the smell of the soil after rain? For the juicy peaches that melt in your mouth? For the sound of the tumultuous waves when they reach the shore? For the laughter of a child that views the world as a wonder?<br/><br/>Darrow au Andromedus fights for the freedom, the opportunity to live for the above. For an oppressed people that hides in the shadows of the so-called superiors for centuri</span>
  <span id="freeText11357555011677154006" style="display:none"><b>What do you live for? </b><br><br>Money? Fame? Glory? Love? Family? Ambition? <br>For the autumn leaves that rustle under your feet? For the smell of the soil after rain? For the juicy peaches that melt in your mouth? For the sound of the tumultuous waves when they reach the shore? For the laughter of a child that views the world as a wonder?<br><br>Darrow au Andromedus fights for the freedom, the opportunity to live for the above. For an oppressed people that hides in the shadows of the so-called superiors for centuries. But in order to escape the monster, you either hide or fight. And fighting is the path, the painful, bloody, sinister path Darrow chose. Betray your friends. Scheme with your enemies. Rise next to people who stole your everything. Alienate those who genuinely care about you. And in doing so, <b>become the monster yourself</b>. <br><blockquote>
  <b>“We are not our station in life. We are us - the sum of what we've done, what we want to do, and the people who we keep close.” </b>
</blockquote><br>Darrow is a Peerless Scarred now, but he's not even close to his mission; <b>destroy the Society, and the Colours, before the Society destroys him.</b> After an unfortunate incident in the Academy his position is precarious, and Nero au Augustus is ready to renounce him and leave him unprotected against the Bellonas, the powerful family that wants his head on a silver platter. But then the Sons of Ares reemerge, giving him orders too cruel to follow, and Darrow realises that the way to make the Society fall apart is <b>civil war</b>. <br>And so it begins.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1515262675i/24848302._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>“Let him think he owns me. Let him welcome me into his house, so I might burn it down.” </b>
</blockquote><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15839976.Red_Rising__Red_Rising___1_" title="Red Rising (Red Rising, #1) by Pierce Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Red Rising</a> was a superb debut that set the standards for the sequel very high. You all know the dreadful term 'middle book syndrome', right? Well, forget it, because instead of a lame, weak second book, <b>the genious called <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6474348.Pierce_Brown" title="Pierce Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Pierce Brown</a> gave us a masterpiece</b>.<br><br>As the story progressed, and Darrow had to make difficult decisions for the sake of his mission, <b>I mourned him</b>; I mourned every piece of his soul, of his conscience, of the past Darrow he had to sacrifice in order to make Eo's dream come true, and give a future to those who were denied it. Sometimes he was lost beyond redemption, a cocky, brutal Gold that stabbed his friends in the back and led armadas and thousands of people to their death with a simple order. But some other times, those rare moments he chose to trust, to protect the weak, to arm a terrifying giant and make love to the girl who stole his heart, he was a fiery Red. In the end, <b>Darrow is both. The amagalm of two cultures, the weapon to divide only to unite.</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1515262069i/24848098.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>“Rise so high, in mud you lie.” </b>
</blockquote><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18966819.Golden_Son__Red_Rising___2_" title="Golden Son (Red Rising, #2) by Pierce Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Golden Son</a> is focused on <b>war and politics, plots and treason</b> that put you on constant alert. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6474348.Pierce_Brown" title="Pierce Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Pierce Brown</a> imagined and brought to life <b>vivid, heartpounding space battles and massacres</b>, he crafted high-tech spaceships and luscious palaces brimming with poisonous snakes. He introduced radiant new characters -let's take a moment to appreciate Victra and the glorious House Telemanus - and explored old ones, giving them voices and backrounds and motives and actions that shook you to the core. <b>The death toll was extremely high</b>. The nameless lives lost unimaginable. But this <b>battlesong of deviousness and blood</b> was injected with moments of jolly <b>laughter</b> and <b>camaraderie</b> that made your shields crack, and a ray of sunlight crawled into your petrified insides. There were also a couple of scenes so <b>powerful</b> and <b>raw</b>, in their simple gestures and scarce dialogues, that make you sob and <i>feel</i> and want to reach for Darrow and hold his hand. There was <b>grandeur</b> in those scenes. In the entirety of this <b>magnificent</b>, <b>soul-ripping</b> book.<br><blockquote>
  <b>“Hic sunt leones. Here be lions.” </b>
</blockquote><br>But except from lions, there are also jackals. And in kindness, there is malice. Darrow kept friends at arm's length and miscalculated people, only to pay with blood in the astounding, devastating ending that shred my soul to pieces. Please, <i>please</i>, <b>
  <i>please</i>
</b>, read this series. And trust <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6474348.Pierce_Brown" title="Pierce Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Pierce Brown</a> to lead you to a dangerous journey that will stay with you for a while.<br><br>[<a href="http://phantomrin.tumblr.com/tagged/Red+Rising" rel="nofollow noopener">Source of this gorgeous Red Rising fan art</a>]<br><br><a href="http://booknest.eu/reviews/kat/1001-goldenson" rel="nofollow noopener">*You can find this review and more on BookNest!*</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="11357555011677154006" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer2494456965048255942">Rating: 4.5 stars<br/><br/>It's hard to believe that there can be even more action after Red Rising, but lo and behold! My heart breaks for these characters... they have loved and lost so much, but they just keep on fighting for what they believe is right. <br/><br/>It was great spending more time with this crew, and meeting some fantastic new characters, too! I love Darrow's brain - he comes up with the most clever, and often crazy, plans, and it was so much fun (yet stressful) seeing them unfold. <br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/></span>

<div id="review_877168514" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/877168514" />
    <a title="C.G. Drews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews"><img alt="C.G. Drews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1521552918p2/11375137.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/877168514?book_show_action=true">Mar 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="C.G. Drews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="C.G. Drews" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews">C.G. Drews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=reread">reread</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=read-2018">read-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=read-2015">read-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer877168514" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8131139554219685432"><b>READ #2, Jan 2018:</b><br/>I'm going to go ahead and say it: but this book is bloodydamn brilliant. I originally rated it 4 stars and then upped it to 5 because holy shit this book did not hold back. It was complex, smart, twisty, and powerful. And the actual rise in quality of the writing and characters was AMAZING!?? (For starters it was way way less sexist than Red Rising too.)<br/><br/>GAH. I'M IN LOVE.<br/><br/>And rereading was <i>so freaking stressful</i> because I knew what was going down in the end and I just??? I did not</span>
  <span id="freeText8131139554219685432" style="display:none"><b>READ #2, Jan 2018:</b><br />I'm going to go ahead and say it: but this book is bloodydamn brilliant. I originally rated it 4 stars and then upped it to 5 because holy shit this book did not hold back. It was complex, smart, twisty, and powerful. And the actual rise in quality of the writing and characters was AMAZING!?? (For starters it was way way less sexist than Red Rising too.)<br /><br />GAH. I'M IN LOVE.<br /><br />And rereading was <i>so freaking stressful</i> because I knew what was going down in the end and I just??? I did not want???<br /><br />Also Sevro is a nasty little shit and I love him to death.<br /><br />Also 10/10 to the audiobooks, I love this series WAY better listening because my mind actually absorbs what I'm reading because apparently my eyeballs aren't connected to my brain but my ears are. Lovely.<br /><br /><br />*** <b>READ #1, February 2015</b> ***<br /><br /><b>Woah...how do I even begin to talk about this book?!</b> I'm so, so torn. I loved it, but I loved <i>having read it</i>, and not the actual <i>reading</i>. I know I'm weird, but give me a sec to explain. <b>I am two thousand percent in love with Red Rising.</b> I AM. That book made 2013 the best year of my LIFE. I devoured Red Rising. I cried. I shipped. I think I had a small heart attack several times... But Golden Son just didn't live up to my feels of Red Rising. I felt like Golden Son had a completely different tone and vibe. And I didn't like it. <br /><br /><b>I felt Red Rising was really focused on Darrow...but Golden Son was really focused on politics and war.</b> I'm not saying it was badly written at all. In fact, I'm pretty extra sure it was genius. But I'm for books about CHARACTERS. And GS just...wasn't. I feel like my non-loves of this book is very much "it's me not you". As I read I gaped like a codfish at the pure skill it would've taken to write. (I bow to Pierce Brown for sure.) It was excellently written. It was stuffed with complex plots and detailed political climates. It had some skull bashing and blood letting. It had enemies and friends-of-enemies, and maybe-enemies and possible-enemies and EVERYTHING WORRYING YOU CAN THINK OF. <br /><br />My favourite were the tender moments. Like when Darrow went home and spoke to his mum again. :') I was ridiculously feelsy in that scene. Or when Darrow confessed <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ he was a Red to Sevro. OH SEVRO HOW I LOVE THEE. I'm enormously pleased Sevro is half-Red. He's adorable <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Darrow is twenty now (so it's not really a YA book) and he's lost all of the boyishness he ever clung to, but he also is very aware he's turning into a monster. And he doesn't want to! He wants to be kept in check. And there are some really vulnerable moments with Darrow. I feel all squishy. DARROW IS AMAZING. He has the weight of worlds (literally) on his Golden Red shoulders and...and...he's still walking.<br /><br />Well, KINDA. <b>Did I mention there was a wicked awful cliffhanger?</b> THERE IS AND IT HURTS, PEOPLES, IT HURTS. I was on the last 20 pages when I realised it was going to end very, very badly. Betrayal. General nastiness. A bit of beheading. Oh gosh. <br /><br /><b>This book is simultaneously incredible and complex and basically out of my league.</b> I felt like I was drowning read it. I'm not really into hardcore sci-fi....I just don't keep up! So this is all ME and not the book. It's a fantastic book, but I wanted more Darrow. Instead I got pages and pages of political TALK and I was bored. I'm very very keen for Morning Star though because...bloodydamn cliffhanger.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8131139554219685432" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

<div id="review_2971293554" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2971293554" />
    <a title="megs_bookrack" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/48328025-megs-bookrack"><img alt="megs_bookrack" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1532027727p2/48328025.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2971293554?book_show_action=true">Sep 13, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="megs_bookrack" class="user" itemprop="url" name="megs_bookrack" href="/user/show/48328025-megs-bookrack">megs_bookrack</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/24408006-golden-son">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2971293554" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11783325331453502189"><b><i>Golden Son</i> has officially wrecked me.</b> <br/><br/>Checking my pulse now to make sure I'm actually still alive. Status unclear.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1456599771ra/18256333.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Picking up approximately 2-years after the events of <i>Red Rising</i>, we continue to follow our intrepid hero, Darrow au Anadromedus, also known as, The Reaper. <br/><br/>His secret war against the heartless rulers of society, the Golds, rages forth. The ultimate goal of which is to demolish the status quo.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455877873ra/18161777.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Full of the same action-packed, pulse-pounding battle scenes as the first book, this one amps</span>
  <span id="freeText11783325331453502189" style="display:none"><b><i>Golden Son</i> has officially wrecked me.</b> <br><br>Checking my pulse now to make sure I'm actually still alive. Status unclear.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1456599771ra/18256333.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Picking up approximately 2-years after the events of <i>Red Rising</i>, we continue to follow our intrepid hero, Darrow au Anadromedus, also known as, The Reaper. <br><br>His secret war against the heartless rulers of society, the Golds, rages forth. The ultimate goal of which is to demolish the status quo.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455877873ra/18161777.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Full of the same action-packed, pulse-pounding battle scenes as the first book, this one amps up the level of political intrigue. <br><br>It left my head spinning, and yes, that's absolutely a good thing!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441207738ra/16078251.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My favorite part of this continues to be the world-building. Brown has created a <b>dark, dystopian world with all of the brutality of ancient Rome</b>, but in space. <br><br>As we all know, everything is better...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1577722946ra/28689361.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Additionally, the characters are compelling and well-fleshed out. <br><br>Darrow is particularly riveting. I love his evolution as a character and have truly felt for him as he grapples with impossible decisions that ultimately end up haunting him.<br><br>It's hard to lead a revolution. Particularly when you have to keep it hidden. A proverbial snake in the grass, who can he trust with his secrets?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1517434991ra/24976928.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>His pain and joy are visceral. I felt every moment. <br><br>Relationships are continuing to develop and as always, there is a healthy dose of back-stabbing and ruthless betrayals mixed in for good measure.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1577722946ra/28689362.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am really looking forward to moving on with this story. My plan is to continue with the audiobooks. The narrator is Darrow to me. <br><br>They couldn't have selected a better choice! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1531890768ra/25990071.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So well done.<br><br>If you haven't picked up this genre-bending series yet, I cannot recommend it highly enough!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11783325331453502189" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44137919-mikee-readwithmikee"><img alt="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583262285p2/44137919.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1848167181?book_show_action=true">Dec 27, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" href="/user/show/44137919-mikee-readwithmikee">Mikee (ReadWithMikee)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780345539816" href="/book/show/20697410-golden-son">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1848167181" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11515285562035543775"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>❝My son, my daughter, now that you bleed, you shall know no fear, no defeat, only victory. Your cowardice seeps from you. Your rage burns bright. Rise, warrior of Gold, and take with you your Color’s might.❞</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>THAT ENDING. I AM SPEECHLESS. I don't even know what to say. This book was full of surprises. Literally. I did not see any of this coming. This series just keeps getting better and better. You'd think that Golden Son would suffer the "book before the finale" syndrome but NOPE. Not</span>
  <span id="freeText11515285562035543775" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>❝My son, my daughter, now that you bleed, you shall know no fear, no defeat, only victory. Your cowardice seeps from you. Your rage burns bright. Rise, warrior of Gold, and take with you your Color’s might.❞</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />THAT ENDING. I AM SPEECHLESS. I don't even know what to say. This book was full of surprises. Literally. I did not see any of this coming. This series just keeps getting better and better. You'd think that Golden Son would suffer the "book before the finale" syndrome but NOPE. Not even close. Pierce Brown just set us up for one of the most epic finales ever. I just know it.<br /><br />My poor Darrow. My heart breaks for him so much. He's lost so much and he's been betrayed so many times. I can't handle this. All my favorite characters, everyone, is NOT safe and it scares me so much. Please protect my babies!<br /><br />And let me just say that I ship Darrow and Mustang 1000%. I ship them so much, it literally hurts. Mustang is a goddess and I hope she finally comes to her senses soon!<br /><br />LASTLY, WE NEED TO PROTECT SEVRO AND RAGNAR AT ALL COST. Nobody is worthy of them.<br /><br />I can't even write a proper review because that ending just destroyed me and now I have to go binge read the finale. BYE.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3034856456617278110"><b>5/5</b>★★★★★<br/><br/>What a fun Buddy Read with team Howlers; <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/59458347-petrik' rel='nofollow noopener'>Speedy eye Oppa</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/35431290-tweebs' rel='nofollow noopener'>Whorefart Aga</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/7317186-celeste' rel='nofollow noopener'>Dewi</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes' rel='nofollow noopener'>Minxy</a> & <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/35147071-jenn-the-dark-lord-scribe-house-of-slytheread' rel='nofollow noopener'>Voldemort</a> <br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>'If your heart beats like a drum and your leg's a little wet, it's 'cause the Reaper's come to collect a little debt.'</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><u>
  <b>that ending...... <i>That MOTHERFUCKING ENDING. </i></b>
</u><br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414429059ra/11652975.gif' width='300' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b><br/>I AM<br/>DEAD <br/>BECAUSE<br/>MY <br/>MIND<br/>JUST <br/>EXPLODED<br/><br/>KA <br/><br/>B<br/><br/>O<br/><br/>O<br/><br/>M<br/><br/>! </b><br/><br/>Hear that sound? Relax. it's just the sound of my mind being blown and my brains splattering the walls.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1484126908i/21684176.jpg' width='300' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Holy balls is right folks. How the hell did the author think of su</span>
  <span id="freeText3034856456617278110" style="display:none"><b>5/5</b>★★★★★<br><br>What a fun Buddy Read with team Howlers; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/59458347-petrik" rel="nofollow noopener">Speedy eye Oppa</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/35431290-tweebs" rel="nofollow noopener">Whorefart Aga</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/7317186-celeste" rel="nofollow noopener">Dewi</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes" rel="nofollow noopener">Minxy</a> &amp; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/35147071-jenn-the-dark-lord-scribe-house-of-slytheread" rel="nofollow noopener">Voldemort</a> <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>'If your heart beats like a drum and your leg's a little wet, it's 'cause the Reaper's come to collect a little debt.'</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><u>
  <b>that ending...... <i>That MOTHERFUCKING ENDING. </i></b>
</u><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414429059ra/11652975.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b><br>I AM<br>DEAD <br>BECAUSE<br>MY <br>MIND<br>JUST <br>EXPLODED<br><br>KA <br><br>B<br><br>O<br><br>O<br><br>M<br><br>! </b><br><br>Hear that sound? Relax. it's just the sound of my mind being blown and my brains splattering the walls.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1484126908i/21684176.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Holy balls is right folks. How the hell did the author think of such an awesome ending?!<br><br>Sweet baby Jesus it's been 24 hours since I finished and I need a whole bottle of wine (to myself). This goddamn book has killed me, I am now currently deceased. Sorry but I have to say it again; THAT ENDING.. I have honestly in my whole 24 years of existence, never been so mind blown before. That cliffhanger left me breathless, strained &amp; stressed, as soon as I put this book down I ran into my lounge room like a possessed mad woman and tore book three off the shelf and started straight away. I thought book one was good, book two was even better! *puts on favourite shelf and starts worshipping for eternity*<br><br><b>Warning and an apology in advance for anyone reading this rubbish. I'm actually at a lost for words, so this is just word vomit. I feel like if I vomited out a pile of dog shit it would be coherent &amp; more interesting then this review.</b><br><br><i>“You are but a mortal," Roque whispers in my ear, riding his horse alongside the chariot, as per tradition. <br>"And a whorefart," Servo calls from the other side.<br>"Yes," Roque agrees solemnly. "That too.”</i><br>Did I read that shit correctly or are my eyes deceiving me... A whorefart?! I'm pissing myself &amp; stealing this brilliant saying.<br><br>I'm so glad this surpassed my expectations. I thought I hated space opera turns out I secretly love it, all thanks to this book. I enjoyed this book more then book one, all because it felt more spacey. In book one the competition on Mars felt like Earth to me so it was kinda unoriginal. I'm happy I can't say that about this book, it felt like a proper Sci-Fi. I loved the space ships I loved the pulse weapons I actually just loved everything, the world building was fantastic, the character development (especially Darrow) was so realistic and awesome &amp; it was so exciting the action didn't stop once. I'm also happy to say I've grown use to the first person POV now and it isn't bothering me at all now, I find comfort in Darrows POV for some reason, mainly because I know he is a crazy dude and he will fuck the golds up. So I'm happy to safely say this book was more my cup of tea then book one, it had more fighting &amp; action. We also didn't go through 200 pages of information dumpage. *phew wipes sweat from forehead*<br><br>I couldn't get enough of Darrow in this instalment, it was so refreshing to see him fail &amp; go through hell for the second time. (Yay?)<br><br>Also my baby, my darling, my Sevro. I swear I'm jealous of other women liking him, I love him that much and he isn't even real. There were some moments in this book i truly adored. Like when him and Darrow confess everything to each other what a wonderful heart warming bromance. Also his entrance towards the beginning *heart eyes* I love HIM. *howls at the moon like a mad bitch*<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You're a sinister little shit, aren't you?" Victra asks.<br>"I'm Gold, bitch. What'd you expect? Warm milk and cookies just because I'm pocket sized?”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Also my new second favourite character of the series is.... drum roll please...... The big badass Ragnar, what a cool dude. He is like a space version of the bloody nine. I wanna see him go batshit &amp; kill everyone.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1484184855i/21691086.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Like a sheep invited to a banquet in his honor thrown by wolves.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I literally can't fault this book I'm just so happy, thrilled &amp; impressed with the hottie known as Pierce Brown. Awesome book dude and if you ever see me at a convention prepare yourself. *wink*<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468863721ra/19753740.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Just take all my money Pierce Brown &amp; give me more badassery and keep quenching my blood thirst. Please &amp; thank you.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1484184855ra/21691087.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I do not recommend this book to anyone under the age of 16 no idea why this brutal masterpiece is on the fucking YA shelf. Should be military space opera or just plain old Sci - Fi.<br>Who I do recommend this to is everyone who loves a good blood bath, also I think just everyone on this planet should read this book it's awesome and full of so many unexpected twists. I think you would also enjoy this if your a <b>whorefart</b> like me.<br><br><b>9/10</b></span>

    <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four"><img alt="Robin (Bridge Four)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473392517p2/14105531.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/865845125?book_show_action=true">Feb 26, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Robin (Bridge Four)" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four">Robin (Bridge Four)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=quit-crying-robin">quit-crying-robin</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=bro-mantic">bro-mantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=kick-ass-heroines">kick-ass-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=chick-i-want-to-hang-out-with">chick-i-want-to-hang-out-with</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=o-captain-my-captain">o-captain-my-captain</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=4-5-stars">4-5-stars</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer865845125" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7666873692995752996">Re-read with some of my Glorydamn friends at <b>
  <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148164-buddies-books-and-baubles' rel='nofollow noopener'>Buddies Books and Baubles</a>
</b> because there was a lot of stuff that went down in this and I need to relive it all going into Morning Star.<br/><br/>I'm glad I reread this since I had forgotten so much of what happened early on this this book. And even though I knew what was going to happen at the end and I knew it was coming and I was waiting for it to get there it still affected me so deeply and hurt just as much if not more than the first time.<br/><br/>I'm pretty sure</span>
  <span id="freeText7666873692995752996" style="display:none">Re-read with some of my Glorydamn friends at <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148164-buddies-books-and-baubles" rel="nofollow noopener">Buddies Books and Baubles</a>
</b> because there was a lot of stuff that went down in this and I need to relive it all going into Morning Star.<br><br>I'm glad I reread this since I had forgotten so much of what happened early on this this book. And even though I knew what was going to happen at the end and I knew it was coming and I was waiting for it to get there it still affected me so deeply and hurt just as much if not more than the first time.<br><br>I'm pretty sure Pierce Brown just stuck a knife through my heart all over again.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492495446i/22521857._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The good news is that I now only have to wait 4 days to see how the rest of this bloodydamn series plays out...instead of the year I had to wait before.<br><br><b>THE GOLDS ARE GOING DOWN</b><br><br><b>Original Review Dec 2014</b><br><br><b>4.5 GLORYDAMN Stars</b><br><br>Everyone is comparing this book/series to Hunger Games, Enders Game and Game of Thrones well I say screw that….<b>THIS IS THE SERIES OTHERS WILL COMPARE THEIR BOOKS TO</b>. <br><br><pre>Step 1 - Read or Reread (trust me on this,<br> unless you read it in the last few<br> months) Red Rising<br>Step 2 - Find a quiet space and time to immerse <br> yourself in this book. Once you start<br> you will not want to stop.<br>Step 3 - Gather snacks, comfortable clothes,<br> pillows and blankets. You are not<br>	 going to want to get up for anything <br>Step 4 - Make sure to have your highlighter<br> ready there are so many great lines to<br> mark.<br>Step 5 - <b>READ ALL THE WORDS!!!!!</b></pre><br><a href="http://s1267.photobucket.com/user/FionaFixit/media/breakthechians_zps303ecfad.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418793731i/12899979._SX540_.png" alt=" photo breakthechians_zps303ecfad.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Pierce Brown has done it again and created fantastic, complicated characters in a new world with danger, betrayal, humor, epic battles, political intrigue and awesomeness around every corner. I had inklings and theories and suppositions throughout the entire book and I got a few right but most of the time I was so wrong and <b>I loved all the surprises. </b><br><br>I’m not going to give any spoilers because I want everyone to be as surprised and blown away as I was by events as they happen.<br><br><a href="http://s1267.photobucket.com/user/FionaFixit/media/DarrowQuote_zps6a3b15c2.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418794240i/12901376._SX540_.gif" alt=" photo DarrowQuote_zps6a3b15c2.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Darrow</b> - It has to be hard living in the middle of the enemy and not forgetting from time to time why you are there. He has a lot of personal growth to go through as he tries to find his way in this world with all the Golds. He will take some chances and I will cross my fingers that they all work out. Darrow is struggling to become the man he needs to be to lead his people out of a slavery they do not even know they are in and stumbling along the way I hold my breath rooting for him to win at every instance. <br><br><a href="http://s1267.photobucket.com/user/FionaFixit/media/redbackquote_zps1441a927.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418794240i/12901377._SX540_.png" alt=" photo redbackquote_zps1441a927.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>If you felt the first book was Intense well I have to say that I believe this book to be even more so. But there are still so great characters to add humor and a human face to all of the events. I love Darrow and Mustang I ship them with the intensity of a thousand stars….but <b>SERVO</b> always steals the show for me.<br><br>Do you like bromances? I love them. True friendships that withstand anything and everything. Servo is the best friend a man like Darrow could have and he is even more crazy and fantastic in this book.<br><br>There are so many great characters in this book, some from the past and more introduced. Plus there was new interesting and exciting information on some of the other colors that we haven’t seen yet. I was drawn into the story and world even more this time around and it was bloodydamn great. New characters to love…RAGNAR and new characters to hate…______ (not telling). <br><br>AND THAT ENDING……What will I do as I contemplate for the next year how that is going to work out. I am all a twitter with anticipation.<br><blockquote>
  <a href="http://s1267.photobucket.com/user/FionaFixit/media/mind_zps2ca63e41.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418583867i/12841609.jpg" alt=" photo mind_zps2ca63e41.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote><br><i>THANK YOU!!!THANK YOU!!!THANK YOU to Del Rey publishing via Netgalley for the ARC for review</i><br><br></span>

<div id="review_2224457264" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2224457264" />
    <a title="❄️BooksofRadiance❄️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/68538597-booksofradiance"><img alt="❄️BooksofRadiance❄️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1513125058p2/68538597.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2224457264?book_show_action=true">Dec 24, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="❄️BooksofRadiance❄️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="❄️BooksofRadiance❄️" href="/user/show/68538597-booksofradiance">❄️BooksofRadiance❄️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780345539816" href="/book/show/20697410-golden-son">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68538597-booksofradiance?shelf=adult-fantasy-sci-fi">adult-fantasy-sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68538597-booksofradiance?shelf=ya-fantasy-sci-fi">ya-fantasy-sci-fi</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2224457264" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10702093501309386334">3.75⭐️<br/><br/>After the underwhelming and super unsatisfying Red Rising (which started out well then went downhills), Golden Son turned out to be a complete surprise in every aspect but one. And it would’ve been a solid 4⭐️ read, were it not for the characters. <br/><br/> <br/><b>The Plot:</b><br/><br/>Golden Son continues with Darrow’s quest for vengeance and retribution and right off the bat, it started out with some much needed humbling and a vicious learning experience for him, which hyped me up for the rest of the book because th</span>
  <span id="freeText10702093501309386334" style="display:none">3.75⭐️<br /><br />After the underwhelming and super unsatisfying Red Rising (which started out well then went downhills), Golden Son turned out to be a complete surprise in every aspect but one. And it would’ve been a solid 4⭐️ read, were it not for the characters. <br /><br /> <br /><b>The Plot:</b><br /><br />Golden Son continues with Darrow’s quest for vengeance and retribution and right off the bat, it started out with some much needed humbling and a vicious learning experience for him, which hyped me up for the rest of the book because the constant unstoppable successes he’d been having and the whole 'too good to lose' thing was seriously getting far too much and plain unrealistic (the boy desperately needed some lesson in humility). <br /><br />In comparison to RR, almost everything in Golden Son was a step up and I found the setup generally impressive. The stakes were higher, the need for vengeance even greater (though, personally, I didn't buy it), the balance of violence and the action was also a lot more even - with much more entertaining scenes of spaceship battles &amp; combat with advanced weapons. We also find out a bit more about the Sons of Ares as well as the inner workings of the politics of the Golds, which I was pleased about.<br />So, generally, sounds great right? NO. Because while I enjoyed the plot (still could've done with a lot more edge but ima let that slide), my hate for Darrow and the rest of the characters grew a considerable amount.<br /><br /><br /><b>The Characters:</b><br /><br />Heavens, how I hated them! Which I still can’t understand because this book had all the types of characters (layered, flawed and morally-grey) that I'm always drawn to without fail but for some reason, I couldn’t get behind… these bunch.<br /><br /><br /><b>Darrow:</b><br /><br />Darrow — "The young man chosen to be the saviour of his oppressed people on Mars. The secret hero of the Red rebellion" *eyes rolling*. What hero?? All I saw was a know-it-all, endlessly arrogant kid, who quite literally, thinks he's a gift to humanity. If not <i>the</i> gift. <br />The road with him has been a difficult one, to put it mildly. And I will say this with absolute certainty - I would've enjoyed this book (series) a hell of a lot more if it’d been any other character <i>but</i> Darrow. I couldn’t stand him in Red Rising and I hated him even more in here.<br />For starters, and this only made matters worse because I HATE first-person narratives (with a few exceptions), I had endless problems with how he talked about himself and the perpetually smug way in which he interacted with others, or how he'd let it be known that he's "not one to be crossed", like, get over yourself. I got so tired of being inside his head that at some point, I think I succumbed to my rage and simply screamed - 'Just shut up, already!' <br /><br />And those long-winded inner monologues about his constant inner struggles and “emotional distress” about what he’s doing and whether or not he's any different than the people he's trying to destroy. The majority of the book was spent on these constant back and forths with himself - <i>Am I doing the right thing? have I gone too far? what makes me any different than the golds?</i><br />Then in a matter of seconds, he'd contradict himself by going on and on about how <i>this is what has to be done, fortune favours the brave, sacrifices must be made</i>, to then only flip over and repeat the same thing over again after a few more chapters. It was exhausting and I did not care for it one bit, nor did I buy it. <br /><br />I get that this is an attempt to make his character appear more sympathetic despite all the shitty decisions he continues to make but, NO. It did not endear him to me and it only made him seem like an indecisive kid who didn’t know which way was up or... down.<br />Another thing that got under my skin was the lack of subtlety in the “emotional” dialogues between him and the rest of the cast, which I found none of it to be convincing. <br />all I saw in these characters was simply pride, arrogance and the need for control, which left me even more disconnected from them and the plot. <br /><br /><br /><b>Mustang:</b><br /><br />Mustang was… alright, under normal circumstances, I would’ve loved her. She’s an individual, smart, snarky, knows what she wants and stands by her decisions no matter how unpopular they may seem, so I don't understand why I couldn't connect with her. There was something so... exasperating and extremely arrogant about her that really got under my skin.<br />I didn’t hate her, I simply didn’t like her. <br /><br /><br /><b>Sevro:</b><br /><br />Somebody tell me if I've read the same book as everyone else because I don't get the hype here and I feel like the whole appeal was completely lost on me. However, unlike, Mustang, I didn't dislike Sevro nor did I find him annoying in any way. He was actually my favourite character in the book (with the bar so low, however, I question myself whether or not this is a compliment). I just didn’t get… the appeal. Plus, he was barely in the picture and I didn't get the right amount of time with him as I did with the others.<br /><br />As for the rest of the characters, none is worth mentioning. With the exception of Lorn au Arcos, whom I really liked and who also gave me a plethora of reasons to hate Darrow even more. And since I can't get into it without spoiling some things, I'll just wrap this up right now.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10702093501309386334" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1242133341" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1242133341" />
    <a title="Dorreh" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22599584-dorreh"><img alt="Dorreh" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565727363p2/22599584.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1242133341?book_show_action=true">Mar 31, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dorreh" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dorreh" href="/user/show/22599584-dorreh">Dorreh</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780345539816" href="/book/show/20697410-golden-son">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1242133341" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14836417044295114122">Oh wow, holy mother of bloody/gory damn hell on earth, Mars, Venus and Pluto! What did I just read??!!!!!<br/><br/>This book surpassed the first quite evidently. It was clear from the beginning this would be a great book. <br/><br/>The story picked up where the first book ended, but not quite. The story picks up with a several year gap, where the characters have recovered from the institute and are now members of the active society. They have had a chance to mature and become the people they were meant to be. I thi</span>
  <span id="freeText14836417044295114122" style="display:none">Oh wow, holy mother of bloody/gory damn hell on earth, Mars, Venus and Pluto! What did I just read??!!!!!<br /><br />This book surpassed the first quite evidently. It was clear from the beginning this would be a great book. <br /><br />The story picked up where the first book ended, but not quite. The story picks up with a several year gap, where the characters have recovered from the institute and are now members of the active society. They have had a chance to mature and become the people they were meant to be. I think this is what caught me of guard most. The young and relatively naive children of the first book are now the experienced adults with a hidden agenda.<br /><br />The book wasn't enthralling simply because it was exciting and nerve wrecking, but to me the unpredictability was so enticing. Just when you thought all is well, some major disaster strikes. That ending was the biggest plot twist ever. I mean yes I assumed that things wouldn't go so simple and easy, but I definitely did not expect THAT! <br /><br />I have complaints though, so so many! First of all, Roque, really? Kind hearted, faithful, poetic Roque?!?! He of all people should not have been the one to betray everything in the end. And then there was Victra, I mean yes, although I was ship mustang/Darrow, I fell in love with Victra all the same. There was a place in my heart for the feisty girl with a soft spot for the revolutionary trouble maker with a love for the smell of wet stone. I think her end is what outraged me the most in all of this. <br /><br />In reviewing the first book, I compared this to "game of thrones" and this book only proved how right that analogy was. The concept of betrayal and death gives this book a shark edge, one I've only ever seen in GOT. The anticipation of knowing anyone could betray anyone and that anyone could be killed by any other anyone was the true metaphorical experience of waking on a blades edge. It made every page as exciting as the first, and every sentence a plausible death or life decision. <br /><br />There is a general down to earth reality in the characters of this book that captured my attention since book one. It's like they understand that the deeper darker side of them is controlling them more times than not. It lead me to feel for the characters more than I have in most books that I have read. It's gives them a touch of realism that is ever so lacking in modern fiction. There is always darkness, it's just a matter of which side we fight harder to stay on. It's a constant struggle, they are not some magical heroes of morality born into the light, they are human beings struggling to understand what's right. <br /><br />Overall I adored this book, and yes even though I have been giving out a lot of high stars lately, I think this one is probably my favorite book since 2015. Can't wait to finish morning star and see what finally happens!!!!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="14836417044295114122" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer4267227574093854806">Reread: January 2018 ☆☆☆<br/><br/>Well. This is awkward. Reading Golden Son is arduous af.<br/><br/>This installment shifts to a tech-heavy and space-centric sci-fi novel, which feels like a stark contrast in the wake of Red Rising. In truth, I see the continuity for the complete story arc, it is natural for things to expand. It also feels polarizing, and boring.  <i>But that character development tho...</i> I remain here for Sevro. Always. <br/><br/>**Original review below**<br/><br/>☆☆☆☆☆<br/><br/><b> No spoilers and colorful language abound! I receive</b></span>
  <span id="freeText4267227574093854806" style="display:none">Reread: January 2018 ☆☆☆<br><br>Well. This is awkward. Reading Golden Son is arduous af.<br><br>This installment shifts to a tech-heavy and space-centric sci-fi novel, which feels like a stark contrast in the wake of Red Rising. In truth, I see the continuity for the complete story arc, it is natural for things to expand. It also feels polarizing, and boring.  <i>But that character development tho...</i> I remain here for Sevro. Always. <br><br>**Original review below**<br><br>☆☆☆☆☆<br><br><b> No spoilers and colorful language abound! I received this ARC from the publisher in exchange for an honest review. </b><br><b><br></b> <b><a href="http://ericapetiteame.blogspot.com/2014/01/red-rising-by-pierce-brown.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Red Rising Review (Book 1)</a></b> <br><br><a href="http://s1212.photobucket.com/user/PetiteAme/media/Halloween%20Upload/GIFS/anigif_mobile-4810-1418059011-8_zps2vv0qin1.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419795446ra/13127928.gif" alt=" photo anigif_mobile-4810-1418059011-8_zps2vv0qin1.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>The short answer?<br><br><b>No. </b><br><b><br></b> <b>You have absolutely no idea. </b><br><br> In Golden Son, Brown continues to cultivate the heart of this narrative; an ever beating chord of sentiment, perfectly balanced with the gory realities of war. Two years have passed since the academy, and the loyalties forged there are unmercifully tested while Darrow struggles to define himself. A man of juxtaposition, the Reaper, a Golden God with a heart forged by pit viper venom and ensnared by the songs of the Reds, stands at the helm of the revolution.<br><br><br><b>The intricacy and nuisances seamlessly woven into this multi-dimensional plot has left me speechless. </b><br><br>Golden Son reads differently than Red Rising, and I believe this is one of the more notable aspects of this book. Although this may feel disjointing for some readers, it is in fact an accurate transition for Darrow, as he changes, so does his world. I am once again in awe of how satisfying it is to read Darrow's evolution. His steadfast devotion, in combination with his capacity for introspection is a never-ending feast for the reader.<br><br><b>What Brown does with such complexity is provide a balance in all things, a counterpart in equal measure. Love and war, technology and savagery, advancement and archaic sentiment, Darrow and Sevro. It's no secret that Sevro is my favorite, he is the unyielding voice of truth in a pit of silver tongues. I adore his brutal heart and twisted soul. If Darrow is the golden light of the sun, then Sevro is the velvet darkness of space, you cannot have one without the other.</b><br><br>This is a captivatingly rare middle book that will leave you bewildered, heart broken and thirsting for more. It is violent, it is tender, it is brutal, and it will rip you open like only one hell of a book can.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1212.photobucket.com/user/PetiteAme/media/Halloween%20Upload/GIFS/3bba0b0b-5cfc-463b-a2ef-da1fe98510fb_zps0f87fd46.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389413348i/8029249._SX540_.png" alt=" photo 3bba0b0b-5cfc-463b-a2ef-da1fe98510fb_zps0f87fd46.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><br><a href="http://www.ericapetiteame.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397955482i/9350858.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></span>
  <a data-text-id="4267227574093854806" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1577084309" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1577084309" />
    <a title="Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9740056-kyle"><img alt="Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1481754383p2/9740056.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1577084309?book_show_action=true">Mar 11, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kyle" href="/user/show/9740056-kyle">Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9740056-kyle?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1577084309" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7426243987117120128"><div>
  <p>Epic roller coaster ride from start to finish! I'd have given it 6 stars if I could.</p>
  <p>At the end of the first book of this trilogy, Darrow Au Andromedus, after winning the Institutes barbaric challenge, kneels before his enemy and agrees to become his adopted son. The second book in the trilogy begins two years later with Darrow at the head of a fleet of warships battling a simulated war against house Bellona's oldest son Karnus for victory in the graduation test of the Academy.</p>
  <p>I won't sp</p></div></span>
  <span id="freeText7426243987117120128" style="display:none"><div>
  <p>Epic roller coaster ride from start to finish! I'd have given it 6 stars if I could.</p>
  <p>At the end of the first book of this trilogy, Darrow Au Andromedus, after winning the Institutes barbaric challenge, kneels before his enemy and agrees to become his adopted son. The second book in the trilogy begins two years later with Darrow at the head of a fleet of warships battling a simulated war against house Bellona's oldest son Karnus for victory in the graduation test of the Academy.</p>
  <p>I won't spoil even the first chapter for you. But this author knows how to take you from highs to lows to highs to lows and back again. There were times I wanted to scream "Yeah!!!!" and others when I wanted to throw my tablet across the room. I couldn't help but relate with Darrow in the first book and that continued and deepened in the second. The love he has for his friends continues to grow, as he also gains other friends. He feels terrible guilt because he's constantly having to lie to them about who he really is. The guilt eats at him throughout the novel. I thought it made him so real. I think anyone in that situation would feel the same.</p>
  <p>The writing was amazing. When there was betrayal, it came as a shock. When there was a twist or turn, I was surprised that I didn't see it coming. Which is so refreshing! It seems so many authors think they have to foreshadow things. Prepare our fragile hearts for the shock like we can't take it if they don't. I think there is nothing better than reading something and going "BEEEELP!!!" There was enough of that in this book to make it easily my favorites of all time. Seriously, I think I finally read a book that has dislodged <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/375802.Ender_s_Game__The_Ender_Quintet___1_" title="Ender's Game (The Ender Quintet, #1) by Orson Scott Card" rel="nofollow noopener">Ender's Game</a> as my favorite book of all time.</p>
  <p>Grade A, absolutely fantastic material. Definitely a MUST READ!</p>
  <p>To read my review of the other books in this series, use the links below:</p>
  <blockquote>
      Book One: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1577084292" rel="nofollow noopener">Red Rising</a> <br />	 Book Three: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1577084322" rel="nofollow noopener">Morning Star</a> <br /> 
  </blockquote>
</div></span>
  <a data-text-id="7426243987117120128" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1034296720" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1034296720" />
    <a title="Lucia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia"><img alt="Lucia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484242793p2/8837962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1034296720?book_show_action=true">Aug 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lucia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lucia" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia">Lucia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=bookshelves-owned">bookshelves-owned</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=5-stars-read">5-stars-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1034296720" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16793242011075587102"><b>Profound and thought-provoking, this novel will rarely allow you to catch your breath with its fast-paced and nerve-wracking atmosphere. Pierce Brown stayed true to all what made me love <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15839976.Red_Rising__Red_Rising_Saga___1_' title='Red Rising (Red Rising Saga, #1) by Pierce Brown' rel='nofollow noopener'>Red Rising</a> and even upped the game. I couldn't have wished for a better sequel.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418239121i/12719265.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>"For seven hundred years, my people have been enslaved without voice, without hope. Now I am their sword."</i>
</blockquote><br/>In Golden Son, Darrow continues in his quest of infiltrating into Society ruled by Golds, so he can gain freedom for his peo</span>
  <span id="freeText16793242011075587102" style="display:none"><b>Profound and thought-provoking, this novel will rarely allow you to catch your breath with its fast-paced and nerve-wracking atmosphere. Pierce Brown stayed true to all what made me love <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15839976.Red_Rising__Red_Rising_Saga___1_" title="Red Rising (Red Rising Saga, #1) by Pierce Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Red Rising</a> and even upped the game. I couldn't have wished for a better sequel.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418239121i/12719265.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"For seven hundred years, my people have been enslaved without voice, without hope. Now I am their sword."</i>
</blockquote><br>In Golden Son, Darrow continues in his quest of infiltrating into Society ruled by Golds, so he can gain freedom for his people. What used to be life to death "game" between students is now even deadlier real life fight that touches all Colors in Solar System. This sequel had different pace, setting and feel than its predecessor, yet I knew I was reading the same story. And I loved it even more.<br><br><b>Characters.</b> Depiction and development of characters in this series is outstanding and after reading this book I truly believe that Pierce Brown knows no bounds when it comes to creating fascinating characters. Character-wise, I learnt my lesson in first book - do not get attached. Because besides action, philosophy and politics; this novel is full of deceits, twists and betrayals. What happens when lines between friends and enemies are blurred? Whom can Darrow really trust?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418240462i/12719535.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Writing</b> style has this special melancholic and gutsy quality into it. It fits Darrow's character perfectly. It feels like it truly mirrors his deepest thoughts and moods without any sort of prettification or reserves. It's probably main reason why I feel so connected to Darrow, why I love his character so much. His souls is stripped bare on the pages of this novel, his personality hardened by the life-events he had to go through and it's up to readers to decide whether they accept Darrow the way he is or not. Author does not make excuses. And author definitely does not shy away from despair, brutality and all forms of raw emotions when telling Darrow's story.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Were I still the man Eo knew, I would have stood frozen in horror. But that man is gone. I mourn his passing every day."</i>
</blockquote><br><b>Storytelling.</b> Pierce Brown excels at it and he secured top place among my favorite authors with his madly <b>bloodydamn</b> good storytelling skills. There is nothing I love more than author's ability to completely consume my thoughts and transfer me into the world he creates on the pages of his novel so I feel like I am right there experiencing everything together with the characters. Pierce Brown achieved that with Red Rising and now with the Golden Son as well. I have never read better thought-out story with such an attention to minor details than this one and I can't wait to find out what has Mr. Brown prepared for us in the final book of this phenomenal trilogy!<br><br><i>*ARC provided by publisher as an exchange for honest review*</i><br><br>MORE REVIEWS ON MY BLOG <a href="http://readingismybreathing.blogspot.cz/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b>Reading Is My Breathing</b>
</a></span>

Who can Darrow trust as his journey to destroy his corrupt society continues? <i>Golden Son</i> is a jaw-dropping, fast paced addition to the <b>Red Rising Trilogy</b>, full of intrigue, courage and fast-paced action that left my heart pounding. <br/><br/><i>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1772072187" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer11717635283194703935"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“They say a kingdom divided against itself cannot stand. They made no mention of the heart.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>This is more of a 2 1/2 stars and I enjoyed it <i>slightly</i> more than the previous book. Friends please don't kill me, I tried, but I just can't find myself to love it. D:<br/><br/><b>Dw, there will be no spoilers in my review.</b> I won't be talking about the plot or anything bc then that will spoil those of you who haven't read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15839976.Red_Rising__Red_Rising___1_' title='Red Rising (Red Rising, #1) by Pierce Brown' rel='nofollow noopener'>Red Rising</a>.<br/><br/>I tried so hard and I had so much hope I would end up liking this bc of </span>
  <span id="freeText11717635283194703935" style="display:none"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“They say a kingdom divided against itself cannot stand. They made no mention of the heart.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>This is more of a 2 1/2 stars and I enjoyed it <i>slightly</i> more than the previous book. Friends please don't kill me, I tried, but I just can't find myself to love it. D:<br><br><b>Dw, there will be no spoilers in my review.</b> I won't be talking about the plot or anything bc then that will spoil those of you who haven't read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15839976.Red_Rising__Red_Rising___1_" title="Red Rising (Red Rising, #1) by Pierce Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Red Rising</a>.<br><br>I tried so hard and I had so much hope I would end up liking this bc of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/35147071-jenn-the-dark-lord-scribe-house-of-slytheread" rel="nofollow noopener">PEOPLE</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes" rel="nofollow noopener">PEOPLE</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/35431290-tweebs" rel="nofollow noopener">PEOPLE</a> were tellesing me this gets so much better and I'm just sittin' there like <i>when???</i> I don't know why, but like I just didn't like this, despite being told the series gets "much better" as it goes on. Clearly, it didn't for me, but I still have this tiny thing called hope that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18966806.Morning_Star__Red_Rising___3_" title="Morning Star (Red Rising, #3) by Pierce Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Morning Star</a> will be <i>better.</i> <s>10/10 won't bc like if I disliked the first two books then I definitely ain't likin' the third.</s><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1485366132ra/21808498.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>※As I've said so many times in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1688907835?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">my review</a> for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15839976.Red_Rising__Red_Rising___1_" title="Red Rising (Red Rising, #1) by Pierce Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Red Rising</a>, it was extremely boring for me. I don't know why, but I just can't seem to be hooked into this series and no matter how hard I push myself to <i>enjoy</i> it, I just fucking can't bc I'm dying of boredom. I just wanted to dnf this so hard and never pick it up and pretend I never read this series but like,,, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/35147071-jenn-the-dark-lord-scribe-house-of-slytheread" rel="nofollow noopener">PEOPLE</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes" rel="nofollow noopener">PEOPLE</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/35431290-tweebs" rel="nofollow noopener">PEOPLE</a>. I wasn't hooked, I didn't find anything interesting and it was excruciatingly boring okay? Okay. ○Like all <i>I</i> read about is a dude living some other life bc of his wife's <i>dream</i>, but he actually doesn't do anything. <br><br>※GIVE ಠ_ಠ ME ಠ_ಠ SOME ಠ_ಠ MORE ಠ_ಠ BRUTAL ಠ_ಠ FUCKING ಠ_ಠ DYING. Yo, I be seein' reviews of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/35147071-jenn-the-dark-lord-scribe-house-of-slytheread" rel="nofollow noopener">PEOPLE</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes" rel="nofollow noopener">PEOPLE</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/35431290-tweebs" rel="nofollow noopener">PEOPLE</a> and other people saying there's so much death (which there is) and it's bloody and murderous and there's this human called @me™ who's just like,, <i>where???</i> <b>Yes, there was death</b>, but I wanted the gory descriptions of it. I wanted Darrow fucking riping off their heads as blood dripped and that shit ya'know? Gawd, I am so bloodthirsty, but like,, ¯\_(ツ)_/¯ The only thing that I liked about these books were the mother fucking brutal ass deaths and even that wasn't satisfying enough for me. Obvs, I have some high standards which this book failed to meet. <br><br>※There's this guy named <i>Sevro</i> in this book which literally almost everyone is trash for and then <i>there's me™</i>, who does not get this <i>Sevro</i> hype either and at this point y'all who've read are probably wondering if I'm good in the head. Even in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15839976.Red_Rising__Red_Rising___1_" title="Red Rising (Red Rising, #1) by Pierce Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Red Rising</a>, I couldn't really care for him. I was hoping to y'know become <i>trash</i> for him like all the other <i>normal people</i>,, but like, <i>no</i>. Sure he's cool and all, but I don't see anything about him that makes him stand out so much. <br><br>●Also, I'm kind of sad that sweaty, hot piss™ wasn't mentioned that much. Whenever I read those words in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15839976.Red_Rising__Red_Rising___1_" title="Red Rising (Red Rising, #1) by Pierce Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Red Rising</a>, I legit laughed out loud and then said hot sweaty piss aloud in my house. lmao i have issues. <br><br>*also, I hated Mustang and Darrow as a couple, like no thank you, goodbye. <br><br>Overall,,, this did not meet my expectations and high standards. I am disappointed and ready to die.</span>
